<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицеп.html>прице́п</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pricép</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицеп.html>прице́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицеп.html>прице́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицеп.html>прице́пов</a></b>)

***прицепившийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прицепившийся.html>прицепи́вшийся</a> (19546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицепившийся.html>прицепи́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pricepívšijsja</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прицепить.html>прицепи́ть</a> (13637)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-цепи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-cepítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прицепить.html>прицепи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pricepítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прицепля́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hitch <i>(to)</i>, to hook <i>(on to)</i>, <i>(railroad cars)</i> to couple <i>(to)</i>, <i>(locomotive)</i> to tie on <i>(to)</i>, to make fast <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(brooch, bow etc)</i> to pin <i>(on to)</i>, to fasten <i>(to)</i>, to tack <i>(to)</i>, to tag <i>(on to)</i></li></ol>

***причалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причалить.html>прича́лить</a> (23254)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ча́лить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čálitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причалить.html>прича́лить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričálitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прича́ливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to moor, to land</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>  to tie up (at), to moor (to)</li></ol>

***причастие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a> (27771)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">častʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">part</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μετοχή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metokhḗ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">participium</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričástije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стий</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастный.html>прича́стный</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> participle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">субстантиви́рованное <b><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">substantivírovannoje <b>pričástije</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">substantivized participle (participle that functions as a noun)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">religion</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> communion; Eucharist (ceremony, sacrament, or substances)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастный.html>прича́стный</a> (10566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pričástije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причастный.html>прича́стный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričástnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>participating, concerned, involved, privy
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:причастный.html>прича́стным</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bytʹ <b>pričástnym</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to participate; be involved; be privy; be an accessory</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>participial
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:причастный.html>прича́стный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оборот.html>оборо́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pričástnyj</b> oborót</i> ― <span class="e-translation">participial construction</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***причем.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причем.html>причём</a> (906)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причем.html>причём</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričóm</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>moreover, and, at that, with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:причем.html>причём</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:известный.html>изве́стно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pričóm</b> izvéstno, što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it being known that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:причем.html>причём</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>них</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наполненный.html>напо́лнен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:различный.html>разли́чным</a> конте́нтом</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pričóm</b> káždyj iz nix napólnen razlíčnym kontɛ́ntom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with each of them being filled with a different content.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Usually not translated, but a following finite verb form is often translated as a present participle.
</p>

***причесавший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причесавший.html>причеса́вший</a> (11836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чесать.html>чеса́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">česátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to edit, to polish, to touch up, to smooth out, to doctor

***причислить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причислить.html>причи́слить</a> (21657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:числить.html>чи́слить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">číslitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причислить.html>причи́слить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričíslitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причислять.html>причисля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to add on <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to reckon <i>(among, in)</i>, to number <i>(among)</i>, to rank <i>(among, with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:причислить.html>причи́слить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лик.html>ли́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>святы́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pričíslitʹ</b> k líku svjatýx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to canonize</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to attach <i>(to)</i></li></ol>

***причислять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причислять.html>причисля́ть</a> (27832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причислить.html>причи́слить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pričíslitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причислять.html>причисля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričisljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причислить.html>причи́слить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>to add on <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to reckon <i>(among, in)</i>, to number <i>(among)</i>, to rank <i>(among, with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:причислять.html>причисля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лик.html>ли́ку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:святой.html>святы́х</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pričisljátʹ</b> k líku svjatýx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to canonize</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to attach <i>(to)</i></li></ol>

***причитание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причитание.html>причита́ние</a> (24276)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причитать.html>причита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pričitátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lament, wail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причитание.html>причита́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričitánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причитание.html>причита́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причитание.html>причита́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причитание.html>причита́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>lamentation, wail</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причитать.html>причита́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričitátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to lament <i>(for, over)</i>, to bewail, to keen <i>(over)</i></li></ol>

***причитаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:причитаться.html>причита́ться</a> (15595)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:читать.html>чита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:причитаться.html>причита́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pričitátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be due
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:причитаться.html>причита́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>две</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сячи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">za rabótu jemú <b>pričitájetsja</b> dve týsjači rubléj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">two thousand roubles are due to him for his work; he is to get two thousand roubles for his work</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:причитаться.html>причита́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сто.html>сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s vas <b>pričitájetsja</b> sto rubléj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">you have one hundred roubles to pay</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:причитаться.html>причита́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ну</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">skólʹko s vas ješčó <b>pričitájetsja</b> za mašínu?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">how much is still due on your car?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:причитаться.html>причита́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s tebjá <b>pričitájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"> you owe me a drink</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
